Only valid in classic.<n/><n/>!passive [<builder-name> or "none"]<n/>Assigns player the typed passive or the passive of a selected builder.<n/>example: !passive ghost (assigns the Cloaking builder passive)<n/><n/>!pause (alias: !freeze)<n/>Pauses the game (permits building during build phase).<n/><n/>!unpause (alias: !resume, !unfreeze)<n/>Unpauses the game.<n/><n/>!timer <seconds> [default]<n/>Set the wave countdown timer to the specified number of seconds.<n/>If default is specified, it'll also update all future wave times.<n/><n/>!giveto <number><n/>Gives the selected unit to the specified player number.<n/><n/>!vision<n/>Toggle fog of war across entire map.<n/><n/>!adrenaline<n/>Toggle adrenaline mode<n/><n/>!mutator <off|mutator-name> [<start wave> <stop wave>]<n/>Toggles the named mutator or, if off, disables all activated mutators.<n/>Current mutators: Battle_Hardened, Heavy_Fog, Mini_Bosses, Necrotic_Hordes, Rapid_Growth, Unbearable_Heat, Winter_Chill<n/><n/>!resources<n/>Equivalent to !minerals 100000, !gas 100000, !supply 200.<n/><n/>!minerals <number><n/>Sets player minerals to number provided.<n/><n/>!gas <number><n/>Sets player gas to number provided.<n/><n/>!supply <number><n/>Sets player supply to number provided.<n/><n/>!income <number><n/>Sets player income to number provided.<n/><n/>!level <number [0-40]><n/>Sets player level to number provided.<n/><n/>!experience <number> (alias: !xp, !exp)<n/>Sets player experience to number provided.<n/><n/>!damage <amount><n/>Immediately applies specified amount of damage to the selected unit.<n/><n/>!kill<n/>Immediately kills the selected unit.<n/><n/>!killtype<n/>Immediately kills all units matching the type and player of the selected unit(s).<n/><n/>!teleport<n/>Teleport all units to the center.<n/><n/>!remove <number><n/>Immediately removes the specified player number from the game.<n/><n/>!workers <increases [0-30]> <upgrades [0-5]><n/>Sets refinery upgrades to specified increases and upgrades.<n/><n/>!killtowers<n/>Removes all player towers.<n/><n/>!instant<n/>Toggles gas worker/speed upgrades completing instantly.<n/><n/>!retry<n/>Restart the current wave (resources not reset).<n/><n/>!restart<n/>Returns game to starting conditions.<n/><n/>!reset_ss<n/>Resets all Security System upgrades.<n/><n/>!freedom<n/>Allows builders to move anywhere.<n/><n/>!set <hp|energy|shields> <amount> (alias: !hp, !maxhp, etc)<n/>Sets the designated statistics on selected units.<n/><n/>!sticky [<wave>]<n/>Toggles sticky mode which locks the current (or provided) wave for easy replay.<n/><n/>!reflex<n/>Toggles reflex mode which makes teams receive their own sends<n/><n/>!state <save|load> <slot [0-9]><n/>Stores or restores a build layout from the bank based on slot ID<n/>Note: !state does not accurately track unit costs, supply, or value<n/><n/>!state <import|export> [<slot 0-9> | importString]<n/>Restores a build layout or serializes one for sharing<n/>Note:
